(** * Display Map Category
    Contents:
    - add display map as a subclass of morphisms [display_map_class C]
    - add an interpretation as a subcategory of [codomain C]
    - show that this subcategory is a cleaving [display_map_cleaving]
    - define the inclusion functor [ι : display_map_cat D ⇒ disp_codomain C]
    - define the map between display maps [map_dispmap D D']
    - show that given a Display Map Category we can construct a corresponding Comprehension Category
    - show that given a functor between display map categories, we can construct a pseudo map between the corresponding comprehension categories
    - show the same for natural transformations
 *)

(** ** Display Map *)
Definition display_map_class_data (C : category) : UU :=
  ∏ a b : C, a --> b -> hProp.
Definition display_map_class_data_to_fun {C} {a b} (D : display_map_class_data C) : a --> b -> hProp := D a b.

display_map_class_data_to_fun does not respect the
uniform inheritance condition.
[uniform-inheritance,coercions,default]



C: category
isaset (display_map_class_data C)


C: category
isaset (display_map_class_data C)

x: C
isaset (∏ b : C, C ⟦ x, b ⟧ → hProp)

  
C: category
x, y: C
isaset (C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → hProp)

  
C: category
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
isaset hProp

  exact isasethProp.
Qed.

Definition has_map_pullbacks {C : category} (D : display_map_class_data C) : UU :=
  ∏ (a b c : C) (f : b --> a) (d : c --> a),
    D _ _ d -> ∑ (p : Pullback d f), D _ _ (PullbackPr2 p).


C: univalent_category
isPredicate has_map_pullbacks


C: univalent_category
isPredicate has_map_pullbacks

isaprop (∑ p : Pullback g f, D p y (PullbackPr2 p))

Definition display_map_class (C : category) : UU :=
  ∑ (D : display_map_class_data C), has_map_pullbacks D.

Definition display_map_class_to_data {C : category} (D : display_map_class C) : display_map_class_data C := pr1 D.
Coercion display_map_class_to_data : display_map_class >-> display_map_class_data.


C: category
D: display_map_class C
a, b: C
isPredicate (λ x : C ⟦ a, b ⟧, pr1 D a b x)


C: category
D: display_map_class C
a, b: C
isPredicate (λ x : C ⟦ a, b ⟧, pr1 D a b x)

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
a, b: C
f: C ⟦ a, b ⟧
isaprop (pr1 D a b f)
 apply (pr2 (pr1 D a b f)).
Qed.

∏ x y : C,
(∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, x ⟧), pr1 D y0 x f)
→ (∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f)
  → C ⟦ x, y ⟧ → UU

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y: C
dx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
dy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
UU

  exact (∑ df : pr1 dx --> pr1 dy, df · pr12 dy = pr12 dx · f).
Defined.

C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x y z : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, x ⟧), pr1 D y0 x f0)
(yy : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f0)
(zz : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, z ⟧), pr1 D y0 z f0),
(∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
 df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)
→ (∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
   df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g)
  → ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 zz ⟧,
    df · pr12 zz = pr12 xx · (f · g)

C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x y z : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(xx : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, x ⟧), pr1 D y0 x f0)
(yy : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f0)
(zz : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, z ⟧), pr1 D y0 z f0),
(∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
 df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)
→ (∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
   df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g)
  → ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 zz ⟧,
    df · pr12 zz = pr12 xx · (f · g)
 
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
xx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
yy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
zz: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, z ⟧), pr1 D y z f
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
gg: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g
∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 zz ⟧,
df · pr12 zz = pr12 xx · (f · g)

    
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
xx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
yy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
zz: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, z ⟧), pr1 D y z f
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
gg: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g
pr1 ff · pr1 gg · pr12 zz = pr12 xx · (f · g)

    abstract (
      rewrite <- assoc; rewrite (pr2 gg), assoc, (pr2 ff);
      symmetry; exact (assoc _ _ _)).
Defined.

p: f = g
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 dx₁, pr1 dx₂ ⟧,
df · pr12 dx₂ = pr12 dx₁ · f
transportf
  (λ _ : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧, C ⟦ pr1 dx₁, pr1 dx₂ ⟧) p
  (pr1 ff) = pr1 ff

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x₁, x₂: C
dx₁: ∑ (y : C) (d : C ⟦ y, x₁ ⟧), pr1 D y x₁ d
dx₂: ∑ (y : C) (d : C ⟦ y, x₂ ⟧), pr1 D y x₂ d
f, g: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
p: f = g
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 dx₁, pr1 dx₂ ⟧,
df · pr12 dx₂ = pr12 dx₁ · f
idfun (C ⟦ pr1 dx₁, pr1 dx₂ ⟧) (pr1 ff) = pr1 ff

  reflexivity.
Qed.


C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y: C
dx: display_map_cat_data D x
dy: display_map_cat_data D y
f, g: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
p: f = g
ff: dx -->[ f] dy
pr1 (transportf (mor_disp dx dy) p ff) = pr1 ff


C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y: C
dx: display_map_cat_data D x

f, g: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
p: f = g
ff: dx -->[ f] dy
pr1 (transportf (mor_disp dx dy) p ff) = pr1 ff

  exact (transportf_display_map _ _).
Qed.


C: category

pr1
  (transportb
     (λ H : C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧,
      ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 dx₁, pr1 dx₂ ⟧,
      df · pr12 dx₂ = pr12 dx₁ · H) p ff) = pr1 ff

C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
yy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
identity (pr1 xx) · pr1 ff,,
disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x x y (identity x) f xx
  xx yy
  (identity (pr1 xx),,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof C D x xx) ff =
transportb (mor_disp xx yy) (id_left f) ff
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
xx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
yy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
pr1 ff · identity (pr1 yy),,
disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y y f (identity y) xx
  yy yy ff
  (identity (pr1 yy),,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof C D y yy) =
transportb (mor_disp xx yy) (id_right f) ff
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y, z, w: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, w ⟧
xx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
yy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
zz: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, z ⟧), pr1 D y z f
ww: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, w ⟧), pr1 D y w f
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
gg: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g
hh: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 zz, pr1 ww ⟧,
df · pr12 ww = pr12 zz · h
pr1 ff · (pr1 gg · pr1 hh),,
disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y w f (g · h) xx yy
  ww ff
  (pr1 gg · pr1 hh,,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D y z w g h yy zz ww
     gg hh) =
transportb (mor_disp xx ww) (assoc f g h)
  (pr1 ff · pr1 gg · pr1 hh,,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x z w (f · g) h xx
     zz ww
     (pr1 ff · pr1 gg,,
      disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y z f g xx yy
        zz ff gg) hh)
C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x y : C) (f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(xx : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, x ⟧), pr1 D y0 x f0)
(yy : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f0),
isaset
  (∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
   df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)

ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
identity (pr1 xx) · pr1 ff,,
disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x x y (identity x) f xx
  xx yy
  (identity (pr1 xx),,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof C D x xx) ff =
transportb (mor_disp xx yy) (id_left f) ff

C: category

xx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f

zz: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, z ⟧), pr1 D y z f
ww: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, w ⟧), pr1 D y w f
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
gg: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g
hh: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 zz, pr1 ww ⟧,
df · pr12 ww = pr12 zz · h

disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y w f (g · h) xx yy
  ww ff
  (pr1 gg · pr1 hh,,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D y z w g h yy zz ww
     gg hh) =

  (pr1 ff · pr1 gg · pr1 hh,,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x z w (f · g) h xx
     zz ww
     (pr1 ff · pr1 gg,,
      disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y z f g xx yy
        zz ff gg) hh)
 
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y, z, w: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
h: C ⟦ z, w ⟧
xx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
yy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
zz: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, z ⟧), pr1 D y z f
ww: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, w ⟧), pr1 D y w f
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f
gg: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g
hh: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 zz, pr1 ww ⟧,
df · pr12 ww = pr12 zz · h
pr1
  (pr1 ff · (pr1 gg · pr1 hh),,
   disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y w f (g · h) xx
     yy ww ff
     (pr1 gg · pr1 hh,,
      disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D y z w g h yy zz
        ww gg hh)) =
pr1
  (transportb (mor_disp xx ww) (assoc f g h)
     (pr1 ff · pr1 gg · pr1 hh,,
      disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x z w (f · g) h
        xx zz ww
        (pr1 ff · pr1 gg,,
         disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y z f g xx
           yy zz ff gg) hh))

     (pr1 ff · pr1 gg,,
      disp_map_id_comp_subproof0 C D x y z f g xx yy
        zz ff gg) hh)

    exact (assoc _ _ _).

isaprop (x0 · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)
 exact (homset_property _ _ _ _ _).
Qed.

Definition display_map_cat {C : category} (D : display_map_class C) : disp_cat C
  := (display_map_cat_data D ,, display_map_cat_axioms).

(** *** Proofs about isomorphisms *)
(** These are largely based on proofs from `codomain`. *)


C: category
D: display_map_class C
x: C
dx₁, dx₂: display_map_cat D x
h: z_iso (pr1 dx₁) (pr1 dx₂)
p: pr12 dx₁ = h · pr12 dx₂
z_iso_disp (identity_z_iso x) dx₁ dx₂


C: category
D: display_map_class C
x: C
dx₁, dx₂: display_map_cat D x
h: z_iso (pr1 dx₁) (pr1 dx₂)
p: pr12 dx₁ = h · pr12 dx₂
z_iso_disp (identity_z_iso x) dx₁ dx₂

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C

Definition display_map_pullback
  {C : category} {D : display_map_class C}
  {Γ Γ' : C} (f : Γ' --> Γ)
  (d : display_map_cat D Γ)
  := pr2 D _ _ _ f (pr12 d) (pr22 d).

(** Proof that [display_map_cat] is a [cleaving]. *)

C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C
f: C ⟦ Γ', Γ ⟧
d: display_map_cat D Γ
∑ d' : display_map_cat D Γ', d' -->[ f] d


C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C
f: C ⟦ Γ', Γ ⟧
d: display_map_cat D Γ
∑ d' : display_map_cat D Γ', d' -->[ f] d

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C
f: C ⟦ Γ', Γ ⟧
d: display_map_cat D Γ
display_map_cat D Γ'
C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C
f: C ⟦ Γ', Γ ⟧
d: display_map_cat D Γ
(λ d' : display_map_cat D Γ', d' -->[ f] d) ?pr1

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C
f: C ⟦ Γ', Γ ⟧
d: display_map_cat D Γ
display_map_cat D Γ'
 
C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C
f: C ⟦ Γ', Γ ⟧
d: display_map_cat D Γ
C
C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C

              PullbackSqrCommutes
                (pr1
                   (display_map_pullback f d))))%mor_disp =
t,, Ht
pr11 ((p,, Hp),, Hcomp) =
pr11 ((PullbackArrow (pr1 (display_map_pullback f d))
         (pr1 d'') t (pr12 d'' · g)
         (Ht @ assoc (pr12 d'') g f),,
       PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2
         (pr1 (display_map_pullback f d)) 
         (pr1 d'') t (pr12 d'' · g)
         (Ht @ assoc (pr12 d'') g f)),,
      subtypePath
        (display_map_is_cartesian_subproof C D Γ Γ' f
           d Γ'' g d'')
        (PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1
           (pr1 (display_map_pullback f d)) 
           (pr1 d'') t (pr12 d'' · g)
           (Ht @ assoc (pr12 d'') g f)))

    
C: category
D: display_map_class C
Γ, Γ': C
f: C ⟦ Γ', Γ ⟧
d: display_map_cat D Γ
Γ'': C
g: C ⟦ Γ'', Γ' ⟧
d'': display_map_cat D Γ''
t: C ⟦ pr1 d'', pr1 d ⟧
Ht: t · pr12 d = pr12 d'' · (g · f)
p: C ⟦ pr1 d'', pr1 (display_map_pullback f d) ⟧
Hp: p · PullbackPr2 (pr1 (display_map_pullback f d)) =
pr12 d'' · g
Hcomp: ((p,, Hp) ;; (PullbackPr1
                (pr1
                   (display_map_pullback f d)),,
              PullbackSqrCommutes
                (pr1
                   (display_map_pullback f d))))%mor_disp =
t,, Ht
pr11 ((p,, Hp),, Hcomp) =
pr11 ((PullbackArrow (pr1 (display_map_pullback f d))
         (pr1 d'') t (pr12 d'' · g)
         (Ht @ assoc (pr12 d'') g f),,
       PullbackArrow_PullbackPr2
         (pr1 (display_map_pullback f d)) (pr1 d'') t
         (pr12 d'' · g) (Ht @ assoc (pr12 d'') g f)),,
      subtypePath
        (display_map_is_cartesian_subproof C D Γ Γ' f
           d Γ'' g d'')
        (PullbackArrow_PullbackPr1
           (pr1 (display_map_pullback f d)) (pr1 d'')
           t (pr12 d'' · g)
           (Ht @ assoc (pr12 d'') g f)))

C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ x : C,
(∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f)
→ ∑ y : C, C ⟦ y, x ⟧
C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x y : C)
(xx : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, x ⟧), pr1 D y0 x f)
(yy : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
(∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
 df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)
→ ∑ ff : C ⟦ pr1 (?Goal x xx), pr1 (?Goal y yy) ⟧,
  ff · pr2 (?Goal y yy) = pr2 (?Goal x xx) · f
C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x : C)
(xx : ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f),
?Goal0 x x xx xx (identity x) (id_disp xx) =
transportb (mor_disp (?Goal x xx) (?Goal x xx))
  (functor_id (functor_identity C) x)
  (id_disp (?Goal x xx))
C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x y z : C)
(xx : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, x ⟧), pr1 D y0 x f)
(yy : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f)
(zz : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, z ⟧), pr1 D y0 z f)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(ff : ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
      df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)
(gg : ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 yy, pr1 zz ⟧,
      df · pr12 zz = pr12 yy · g),
?Goal0 x z xx zz (f · g) (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp =
transportb (mor_disp (?Goal x xx) (?Goal z zz))
  (functor_comp (functor_identity C) f g)
  (?Goal0 x y xx yy f ff ;; ?Goal0 y z yy zz g gg)%mor_disp

D: display_map_class C
∏ x : C,
(∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f)
→ ∑ y : C, C ⟦ y, x ⟧
 exact (λ _ d, pr1 d ,, pr12 d).
  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x y : C)
(xx : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, x ⟧), pr1 D y0 x f)
(yy : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧),
(∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
 df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)
→ ∑
  ff : C
       ⟦ pr1
           ((λ (x0 : C)
             (d : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, x0 ⟧),
                  pr1 D y0 x0 f0), pr1 d,, pr12 d) x
              xx),
       pr1
         ((λ (x0 : C)
           (d : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, x0 ⟧),
                pr1 D y0 x0 f0), pr1 d,, pr12 d) y yy)
       ⟧,
  ff
  · pr2
      ((λ (x0 : C)
        (d : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, x0 ⟧),
             pr1 D y0 x0 f0), pr1 d,, pr12 d) y yy) =
  pr2
    ((λ (x0 : C)
      (d : ∑ (y0 : C) (f0 : C ⟦ y0, x0 ⟧),
           pr1 D y0 x0 f0), pr1 d,, pr12 d) x xx) · f
 exact (λ _ _ _ _ _ ff, ff).

C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (x y z : C)

(zz : ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, z ⟧), pr1 D y0 z f)
(f : C ⟦ x, y ⟧) (g : C ⟦ y, z ⟧)
(ff : ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 xx, pr1 yy ⟧,
      df · pr12 yy = pr12 xx · f)

C: category
D: display_map_class C
x, y, z: C
dx: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧), pr1 D y x f
dy: ∑ (y0 : C) (f : C ⟦ y0, y ⟧), pr1 D y0 y f
dz: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, z ⟧), pr1 D y z f
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧
ff: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 dx, pr1 dy ⟧,
df · pr12 dy = pr12 dx · f
gg: ∑ df : C ⟦ pr1 dy, pr1 dz ⟧,
df · pr12 dz = pr12 dy · g
(ff ;; gg)%mor_disp =

  (mor_disp (pr1 dx,, pr12 dx) (pr1 dz,, pr12 dz))
  (functor_comp (functor_identity C) f g)
  (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp
 
C: category

dz: ∑ (y : C) (f : C ⟦ y, z ⟧), pr1 D y z f
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
g: C ⟦ y, z ⟧

df · pr12 dy = pr12 dx · f

df · pr12 dz = pr12 dy · g
pr1 (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp =

  (transportb
     (mor_disp (pr1 dx,, pr12 dx) (pr1 dz,, pr12 dz))
     (functor_comp (functor_identity C) f g)
     (ff ;; gg)%mor_disp)

    reflexivity.
Defined.

  (PullbackSqrCommutes
     (pr1 (display_map_pullback f dx)))

  apply isPullback_Pullback.
Qed.

Qed.

Definition cartesian_ι
  {C : category} (D : display_map_class C)
  : cartesian_disp_functor (functor_identity C) (display_map_cat D) (disp_codomain C)
  := (ι D ,, is_cartesian_ι D).

dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
ι_g: C ⟦ pr1 (ι D x₁ dx₁), pr1 (ι D x₂ dx₂) ⟧
Hsq: ι_g · pr2 (ι D x₂ dx₂) = pr2 (ι D x₁ dx₁) · # (functor_identity C) f
iscontr
  (hfiber
     (λ ff : dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂, (♯ (ι D))%mor_disp ff)
     (ι_g,, Hsq))

Hsq: ι_g · pr2 (ι D x₂ dx₂) = pr2 (ι D x₁ dx₁) · # (functor_identity C) f
∑
cntr : ∑ x : dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂,
       (♯ (ι D))%mor_disp x = ι_g,, Hsq,
∏
t : ∑ x : dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂,
    (♯ (ι D))%mor_disp x = ι_g,, Hsq, t = cntr

(** ** Functor between Display Map Classes *)

Definition preserves_maps {C C' : category} (D : display_map_class C) (D' : display_map_class C') (F : C ⟶ C') :=
  ∏ (a b : C) (d : a --> b), D d -> D' (#F d).


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
isPredicate (preserves_maps D D')


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
isPredicate (preserves_maps D D')

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
isaprop (preserves_maps D D' F)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x: C
isaprop
  ((λ t : C,
    ∏ (b : C) (d : C ⟦ t, b ⟧), D d → D' (# F d)) x)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y: C
isaprop
  ((λ t : C, ∏ d : C ⟦ x, t ⟧, D d → D' (# F d)) y)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
isaprop ((λ t : C ⟦ x, y ⟧, D t → D' (# F t)) f)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
isaprop (D f → D' (# F f))
 
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y: C
f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
isaprop (D' (# F f))

  apply isPredicate_display_map_class.
Qed.

Definition preserves_pullbacks {C C' : category} (D : display_map_class C) (D' : display_map_class C') (F : C ⟶ C') :=
  ∏ (a b c : C) (f : b --> a) (g : c --> a) (_ : D f) (pb : Pullback f g), isPullback (!functor_comp F _ _ @ maponpaths (#F) (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @ functor_comp F _ _).


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
isPredicate (preserves_pullbacks D D')


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
isPredicate (preserves_pullbacks D D')

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
isaprop (preserves_pullbacks D D' F)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x: C
isaprop
  ((λ t : C,
    ∏ (b c : C) (f : C ⟦ b, t ⟧) (g : C ⟦ c, t ⟧),
    D f
    → ∏ pb : Pullback f g,
      isPullback
        (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) f @
         maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
         functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) g)) x)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y: C
isaprop
  ((λ t : C,
    ∏ (c : C) (f : C ⟦ t, x ⟧) (g : C ⟦ c, x ⟧),
    D f
    → ∏ pb : Pullback f g,
      isPullback
        (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) f @
         maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
         functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) g)) y)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y, z: C
isaprop
  ((λ t : C,
    ∏ (f : C ⟦ y, x ⟧) (g : C ⟦ t, x ⟧),
    D f
    → ∏ pb : Pullback f g,
      isPullback
        (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) f @
         maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
         functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) g)) z)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ y, x ⟧
isaprop
  ((λ t : C ⟦ y, x ⟧,
    ∏ g : C ⟦ z, x ⟧,
    D t
    → ∏ pb : Pullback t g,
      isPullback
        (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) t @
         maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
         functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) g)) f)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ y, x ⟧
g: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
isaprop
  ((λ t : C ⟦ z, x ⟧,
    D f
    → ∏ pb : Pullback f t,
      isPullback
        (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) f @
         maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
         functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) t)) g)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ y, x ⟧
g: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
isaprop
  (D f
   → ∏ pb : Pullback f g,
     isPullback
       (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) f @
        maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
        functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) g))
 
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ y, x ⟧
g: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
isaprop
  (∏ pb : Pullback f g,
   isPullback
     (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) f @
      maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
      functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) g))

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
x, y, z: C
f: C ⟦ y, x ⟧
g: C ⟦ z, x ⟧
pb: Pullback f g
isaprop
  ((λ t : Pullback f g,
    isPullback
      (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 t) f @
       maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes t) @
       functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 t) g)) pb)

  apply isaprop_isPullback.
Qed.

Definition is_display_map_class_functor {C C' : category} (D : display_map_class C) (D' : display_map_class C') (F: C ⟶ C') := preserves_maps D D' F × preserves_pullbacks D D' F.


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
isPredicate (is_display_map_class_functor D D')


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
isPredicate (is_display_map_class_functor D D')

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
isaprop (is_display_map_class_functor D D' F)
 
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
isaprop (preserves_maps D D' F)
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
isaprop (preserves_pullbacks D D' F)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
isaprop (preserves_maps D D' F)
 apply isPredicate_preserves_maps.
  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F: C ⟶ C'
isaprop (preserves_pullbacks D D' F)
 apply isPredicate_preserves_pullbacks.
Qed.

Definition preserves_maps_is_display_map_class_functor
  {C C' : category} (D : display_map_class C) (D' : display_map_class C') (F : C ⟶ C')
  : is_display_map_class_functor D D' F -> preserves_maps D D' F := pr1.
Definition preserves_pullbacks_is_display_map_class_functor
  {C C' : category} (D : display_map_class C) (D' : display_map_class C') (F : C ⟶ C')
  : is_display_map_class_functor D D' F -> preserves_pullbacks D D' F := pr2.


C: univalent_category
D₁, D₂: display_map_class C
HF: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
  (functor_identity C)
HG: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₁
  (functor_identity C)
D₁ = D₂

  (functor_identity C)
HG: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₁
  (functor_identity C)
D₁ = D₂

  (functor_identity C)

  (functor_identity C)
isPredicate has_map_pullbacks

  (functor_identity C)
pr1 D₁ = pr1 D₂

 apply isPredicate_has_map_pullbacks.

  (functor_identity C)
pr1 D₁ = pr1 D₂

  (functor_identity C)
HG: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₁
  (functor_identity C)
pr1 D₁ ~ pr1 D₂
 
C: univalent_category

f: C ⟦ x, y ⟧
pr1 D₁ x y f = pr1 D₂ x y f

Definition display_map_class_functor {C C' : category} (D : display_map_class C) (D' : display_map_class C') :=
  ∑ (F: C ⟶ C'), is_display_map_class_functor D D' F.

Definition functor_from_display_map_class_functor {C C' : category} (D : display_map_class C) (D' : display_map_class C') (F : display_map_class_functor D D') : C ⟶ C' := pr1 F.
Coercion functor_from_display_map_class_functor : display_map_class_functor >-> functor.

   functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) f
   :
   pr12 (F pb,,
         # F (PullbackPr1 pb),, # F (PullbackPr2 pb))
   · # F d =
   pr22 (F pb,,
         # F (PullbackPr1 pb),, # F (PullbackPr2 pb))
   · # F f)
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
a, b, c: C₁
d: C₁ ⟦ b, a ⟧
f: C₁ ⟦ c, a ⟧
H: D₁ d
pb: Pullback d f
isPullback
  (! functor_comp F (PullbackPr1 pb) d @
   maponpaths # F (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
   functor_comp F (PullbackPr2 pb) f)
 exact (pr22 F _ _ _ _ _ H pb).
Defined.



C: category
D: display_map_class C
is_display_map_class_functor D D (functor_identity C)


C: category
D: display_map_class C
is_display_map_class_functor D D (functor_identity C)

  exact ((λ _ _ _ tt, tt) ,, (λ _ _ _ _ _ _ pb, isPullback_Pullback pb)).
Defined.

Definition display_map_class_functor_identity
  {C : category} (D : display_map_class C)
  : display_map_class_functor D D
  := (_ ,, is_display_map_class_functor_identity _).


C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
HF₁: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ F₁
HF₂: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃ F₂
is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₃ (F₁ ∙ F₂)


C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
HF₁: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ F₁
HF₂: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃ F₂
is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₃ (F₁ ∙ F₂)

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
HF₁: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ F₁
HF₂: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃ F₂
preserves_maps D₁ D₃ (F₁ ∙ F₂)
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
HF₁: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ F₁
HF₂: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃ F₂
preserves_pullbacks D₁ D₃ (F₁ ∙ F₂)

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
HF₁: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ F₁
HF₂: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃ F₂
preserves_maps D₁ D₃ (F₁ ∙ F₂)
 exact (λ _ _ _ tt, (pr1 HF₂) _ _ _ ((pr1 HF₁) _ _ _ tt)).
  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
HF₁: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ F₁
HF₂: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃ F₂
preserves_pullbacks D₁ D₃ (F₁ ∙ F₂)
 
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F₁: C₁ ⟶ C₂
F₂: C₂ ⟶ C₃
HF₁: is_display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂ F₁
HF₂: is_display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃ F₂
a, b, c: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ b, a ⟧
g: C₁ ⟦ c, a ⟧
tt: D₁ f
pb: Pullback f g
isPullback
  (! (maponpaths # F₂
        (functor_comp F₁ (PullbackPr1 pb) f) @
      functor_comp F₂ (# F₁ (PullbackPr1 pb)) (# F₁ f)) @
   maponpaths (λ f0 : C₁ ⟦ pb, a ⟧, # F₂ (# F₁ f0))
     (PullbackSqrCommutes pb) @
   maponpaths # F₂
     (functor_comp F₁ (PullbackPr2 pb) g) @
   functor_comp F₂ (# F₁ (PullbackPr2 pb)) (# F₁ g))

    apply ((pr2 HF₂) _ _ _ _ _ ((pr1 HF₁) _ _ _ tt) (display_map_class_functor_preserves_pullback (_ ,, HF₁) tt pb)).
Defined.

Definition display_map_class_functor_composite
  {C₁ C₂ C₃ : category}
  {D₁ : display_map_class C₁} {D₂ : display_map_class C₂} {D₃ : display_map_class C₃}
  (F₁ : display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂)
  (F₂ : display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃)
  : display_map_class_functor D₁ D₃
  := (_ ,, is_display_map_class_functor_composite (pr2 F₁) (pr2 F₂)).

(** ** Functor between Display Map Categories *)
(** *** Define how functor `F` acts on the Display Map Category  *)
(** Here, we once again follow the definitions for codomain from [Codomain/CodFunctor.v]. *)

C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
disp_functor_data F (display_map_cat D₁)
  (display_map_cat D₂)


C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
disp_functor_data F (display_map_cat D₁)
  (display_map_cat D₂)

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
∏ x : C₁,
display_map_cat D₁ x → display_map_cat D₂ (F x)
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
(λ Fob : ∏ x : C₁,
         display_map_cat D₁ x
         → display_map_cat D₂ (F x),
 ∏ (x y : C₁) (xx : display_map_cat D₁ x)
 (yy : display_map_cat D₁ y) (f : C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧),
 xx -->[ f] yy → Fob x xx -->[ # F f] Fob y yy) ?pr1

  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
∏ x : C₁,
display_map_cat D₁ x → display_map_cat D₂ (F x)
 exact (λ x yf, F (pr1 yf) ,, #F (pr12 yf) ,, pr12 F _ _ _ (pr22 yf)).
  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
(λ Fob : ∏ x : C₁,
         display_map_cat D₁ x
         → display_map_cat D₂ (F x),
 ∏ (x y : C₁) (xx : display_map_cat D₁ x)
 (yy : display_map_cat D₁ y) (f : C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧),
 xx -->[ f] yy → Fob x xx -->[ # F f] Fob y yy)
  (λ (x : C₁) (yf : display_map_cat D₁ x),
   F (pr1 yf),,
   # F (pr12 yf),,
   (pr12 F) (pr1 yf) x (pr12 yf) (pr22 yf))
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
x₁, x₂: C₁
yf₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
yf₂: display_map_cat D₁ x₂
g: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
hp: yf₁ -->[ g] yf₂
# F (pr1 hp)
· pr12 (F (pr1 yf₂),,
        # F (pr12 yf₂),,
        (pr12 F) (pr1 yf₂) x₂ (pr12 yf₂) (pr22 yf₂)) =
pr12 (F (pr1 yf₁),,
      # F (pr12 yf₁),,
      (pr12 F) (pr1 yf₁) x₁ (pr12 yf₁) (pr22 yf₁))
· # F g

    abstract
      (cbn ;
       rewrite <- !functor_comp ;
       apply maponpaths ;
       exact (pr2 hp)).
Defined.

(♯ (display_map_functor_data F))%mor_disp (id_disp xx) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (display_map_functor_data F x xx)
     (display_map_functor_data F x xx))
  (functor_id F x)
  (id_disp (display_map_functor_data F x xx))

(yy : pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y)
(zz : pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) z) (f : C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : yy -->[ g] zz),
(♯ (display_map_functor_data F))%mor_disp (ff ;; gg) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (display_map_functor_data F x xx)
     (display_map_functor_data F z zz))
  (functor_comp F f g)
  (♯ (display_map_functor_data F) ff ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data
                                             F) gg)%mor_disp

∏ (x y z : C₁) (xx : display_map_cat D₁ x)
(yy : pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y)
(zz : pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) z) (f : C₁ ⟦ x, y ⟧)
(g : C₁ ⟦ y, z ⟧) (ff : xx -->[ f] yy)
(gg : yy -->[ g] zz),
(♯ (display_map_functor_data F))%mor_disp (ff ;; gg) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (display_map_functor_data F x xx)
     (display_map_functor_data F z zz))
  (functor_comp F f g)
  (♯ (display_map_functor_data F) ff ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data
                                             F) gg)%mor_disp
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
x₁, x₂, y₃: C₁
yf₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
yf₂: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) x₂
yf₃: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y₃
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, y₃ ⟧
gp₁: yf₁ -->[ f₁] yf₂
gp₂: yf₂ -->[ f₂] yf₃
(♯ (display_map_functor_data F))%mor_disp (gp₁ ;; gp₂) =
transportb
  (mor_disp (display_map_functor_data F x₁ yf₁)
     (display_map_functor_data F y₃ yf₃))
  (functor_comp F f₁ f₂)
  (♯ (display_map_functor_data F) gp₁ ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data
                                              F) gp₂)%mor_disp

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
x₁, x₂, y₃: C₁
yf₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
yf₂: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) x₂
yf₃: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y₃
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, y₃ ⟧
gp₁: yf₁ -->[ f₁] yf₂
gp₂: yf₂ -->[ f₂] yf₃
pr1
  ((♯ (display_map_functor_data F))%mor_disp
     (gp₁ ;; gp₂)) =
pr1
  (transportb
     (mor_disp (display_map_functor_data F x₁ yf₁)
        (display_map_functor_data F y₃ yf₃))
     (functor_comp F f₁ f₂)
     (♯ (display_map_functor_data F) gp₁ ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data
                                                 F)
                                              gp₂)%mor_disp)

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
x₁, x₂, y₃: C₁
yf₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
yf₂: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) x₂
yf₃: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y₃
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, y₃ ⟧
gp₁: yf₁ -->[ f₁] yf₂
gp₂: yf₂ -->[ f₂] yf₃
# F (pr1 gp₁ · pr1 gp₂) =
pr1
  (transportb
     (mor_disp
        (F (pr1 yf₁),,
         # F (pr12 yf₁),,
         (pr12 F) (pr1 yf₁) x₁ (pr12 yf₁) (pr22 yf₁))
        (F (pr1 yf₃),,
         # F (pr12 yf₃),,
         (pr12 F) (pr1 yf₃) y₃ (pr12 yf₃) (pr22 yf₃)))
     (functor_comp F f₁ f₂)
     (((# F)%cat (pr1 gp₁),,
       display_map_functor_data_subproof C₁ C₂ D₁ D₂ F
         x₁ x₂ yf₁ yf₂ f₁ gp₁) ;; ((# F)%cat (pr1 gp₂),,
                                   display_map_functor_data_subproof
                                     C₁ C₂ D₁ D₂ F x₂
                                     y₃ yf₂ yf₃ f₂ gp₂))%mor_disp)

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
x₁, x₂, y₃: C₁
yf₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
yf₂: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) x₂
yf₃: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y₃
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, y₃ ⟧
gp₁: yf₁ -->[ f₁] yf₂
gp₂: yf₂ -->[ f₂] yf₃
# F (pr1 gp₁ · pr1 gp₂) =
pr1
  (((# F)%cat (pr1 gp₁),,
    display_map_functor_data_subproof C₁ C₂ D₁ D₂ F x₁
      x₂ yf₁ yf₂ f₁ gp₁) ;; ((# F)%cat (pr1 gp₂),,
                             display_map_functor_data_subproof
                               C₁ C₂ D₁ D₂ F x₂ y₃ yf₂
                               yf₃ f₂ gp₂))%mor_disp

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
x₁, x₂, y₃: C₁
yf₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
yf₂: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) x₂
yf₃: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y₃
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, y₃ ⟧
gp₁: yf₁ -->[ f₁] yf₂
gp₂: yf₂ -->[ f₂] yf₃
# F (pr1 gp₁ · pr1 gp₂) =
# F (pr1 gp₁) · # F (pr1 gp₂)

    
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
x₁, x₂, y₃: C₁
yf₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
yf₂: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) x₂
yf₃: pr1 (display_map_cat D₁) y₃
f₁: C₁ ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
f₂: C₁ ⟦ x₂, y₃ ⟧
gp₁: yf₁ -->[ f₁] yf₂
gp₂: yf₂ -->[ f₂] yf₃
# F (pr1 gp₁) · # F (pr1 gp₂) =
# F (pr1 gp₁) · # F (pr1 gp₂)

    apply idpath.
Qed.

 exact (display_map_functor_data F).
  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
(λ FF : disp_functor_data F (display_map_cat D₁)
          (display_map_cat D₂), disp_functor_axioms FF)
  (display_map_functor_data F)
 exact (display_map_functor_axioms F).
Defined.


C: category
D: display_map_class C
x₁, x₂: C
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
dx₁: display_map_cat D x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂
df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂
isPullback (pr2 df) → is_cartesian df


C: category

dx₁: display_map_cat D x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂

isPullback (pr2 df) → is_cartesian df

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x₁, x₂: C
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
dx₁: display_map_cat D x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂
df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂
Hpb: isPullback (pr2 df)
x₃: C
g: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
dx₃: display_map_cat D x₃
dh: dx₃ -->[ g · f] dx₂
∃! gg : dx₃ -->[ g] dx₁, (gg ;; df)%mor_disp = dh
 
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x₁, x₂: C
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
dx₁: display_map_cat D x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂
df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂
Hpb: ∏ (e : C) (h : C ⟦ e, pr1 dx₂ ⟧) (k : C ⟦ e, x₁ ⟧),
h · pr12 dx₂ = k · f
→ ∃! hk : C ⟦ e, pr1 dx₁ ⟧, hk · pr1 df = h × hk · pr12 dx₁ = k
x₃: C
g: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
dx₃: display_map_cat D x₃
dh: dx₃ -->[ g · f] dx₂
∃! gg : dx₃ -->[ g] dx₁, (gg ;; df)%mor_disp = dh
 
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x₁, x₂: C
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
dx₁: display_map_cat D x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂
df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂
x₃: C
g: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
dx₃: display_map_cat D x₃
dh: dx₃ -->[ g · f] dx₂
Hpb: pr1 dh · pr12 dx₂ = pr12 dx₃ · g · f
→ ∃! hk : C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧,
hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh × hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g
∃! gg : dx₃ -->[ g] dx₁, (gg ;; df)%mor_disp = dh

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x₁, x₂: C
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
dx₁: display_map_cat D x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂
df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂
x₃: C
g: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
dx₃: display_map_cat D x₃
dh: dx₃ -->[ g · f] dx₂
Hpb: pr1 dh · pr12 dx₂ = pr12 dx₃ · g · f
→ ∃! hk : C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧,
hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh × hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g
pb:= Hpb (pr2 dh @ assoc (pr12 dx₃) g f): ∃! hk : C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧,
hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh
× hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g
∃! gg : dx₃ -->[ g] dx₁, (gg ;; df)%mor_disp = dh
 
C: category
D: display_map_class C
x₁, x₂: C
f: C ⟦ x₁, x₂ ⟧
dx₁: display_map_cat D x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D x₂
df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂
x₃: C
g: C ⟦ x₃, x₁ ⟧
dx₃: display_map_cat D x₃
dh: dx₃ -->[ g · f] dx₂
Hpb: pr1 dh · pr12 dx₂ = pr12 dx₃ · g · f
→ ∃! hk : C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧,
hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh × hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g
hk: C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧
H1: hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh
H2: hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g
Hunique: ∏
t : ∑ hk : C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧,
    hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh
    × hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g,
t = hk,, H1,, H2
∃! gg : dx₃ -->[ g] dx₁, (gg ;; df)%mor_disp = dh

hk: C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧
H1: hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh
H2: hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g
Hunique: ∏
t : ∑ hk : C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧,
    hk · pr1 df = pr1 dh
    × hk · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g,
t = hk,, H1,, H2
hk': C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧
H2': hk' · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g
H1': ((hk',, H2') ;; df)%mor_disp = dh
isPredicate
  (λ x : C ⟦ pr1 dx₃, pr1 dx₁ ⟧,
   x · pr12 dx₁ = pr12 dx₃ · g)
 exact (λ _, homset_property _ _ _ _ _).

     x₂ f)

     F G x₁ dx₁ ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data
                        (display_map_class_functor_composite
                           F G)) df)%mor_disp

                                         F G x₂ dx₂)%mor_disp =
pr1
  (transportb
     (mor_disp
        (disp_functor_composite_data
           (display_map_functor F)
           (display_map_functor G) x₁ dx₁)
        (display_map_functor_data
           (display_map_class_functor_composite F G)
           x₂ dx₂))
     (nat_trans_ax
        (nat_trans_id
           (functor_composite_data (pr1 F) (pr1 G)))
        x₁ x₂ f)
     (display_map_functor_composite_to_composite_display_map_functor_data
        F G x₁ dx₁ ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data
                           (display_map_class_functor_composite
                              F G)) df)%mor_disp)

D₁: display_map_class C₁

df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂

        F G x₁ dx₁ ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data

                              F G)) df)%mor_disp) =

        (display_map_functor F)

                              F G)) df)%mor_disp) = 
?b

?b =
pr1
  (♯ (disp_functor_composite_data
        (display_map_functor F)
        (display_map_functor G)) df ;; display_map_functor_composite_to_composite_display_map_functor_data
                                         F G x₂ dx₂)%mor_disp

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
D₃: display_map_class C₃
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
G: display_map_class_functor D₂ D₃

dx₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁

pr1
  (display_map_functor_composite_to_composite_display_map_functor_data
     F G x₁ dx₁ ;; ♯ (display_map_functor_data
                        (display_map_class_functor_composite
                           F G)) df)%mor_disp =
pr1
  (♯ (disp_functor_composite_data
        (display_map_functor F)
        (display_map_functor G)) df ;; display_map_functor_composite_to_composite_display_map_functor_data
                                         F G x₂ dx₂)%mor_disp

  
C₁, C₂, C₃: category

D₂: display_map_class C₂

x₁, x₂: C₁

dx₁: display_map_cat D₁ x₁
dx₂: display_map_cat D₁ x₂
df: dx₁ -->[ f] dx₂
identity (G (F (pr1 dx₁)))
· # (pr1 G) (# (pr1 F) (pr1 df)) =
# G (# F (pr1 df)) · identity (G (F (pr1 dx₂)))

  exact (id_left _ @ !id_right _).
Qed.

(** ** Natural Transformation *)
(** Once more we rely on the definition for the codomain display category to define the transformation between two display map categories. *)

  (display_map_functor G)

  (display_map_functor G)

  (display_map_functor G)

         (display_map_functor G),
 disp_nat_trans_axioms b) ?pr1

  (display_map_functor G)
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F, G: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
α: F ⟹ G
y: C₁
xf: display_map_cat D₁ y
α (pr1 xf) · pr12 (display_map_functor G y xf) =
pr12 (display_map_functor F y xf) · α y

    abstract
      (cbn ;
       apply (!(nat_trans_ax α _ _ _))).
  
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F, G: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
α: F ⟹ G
(λ b : disp_nat_trans_data α (display_map_functor F)
         (display_map_functor G),
 disp_nat_trans_axioms b)
  (λ (y : C₁) (xf : display_map_cat D₁ y),
   α (pr1 xf),,
   display_map_nat_trans_subproof C₁ C₂ D₁ D₂ F G α y
     xf)
 abstract (intros y₁ y₂ g xf₁ xf₂ p ;
       use eq_display_map_cat_mor ;
       rewrite (@transportb_display_map_mor _ _ _ _ (display_map_functor F y₁ xf₁)) ;
       apply (nat_trans_ax α _ _ _)).
Defined.

(** ** Corresponding Comprehension Category *)

C: category
D: display_map_class C
comprehension_cat_structure C


C: category
D: display_map_class C
comprehension_cat_structure C

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
disp_cat C
C: category
D: display_map_class C
cleaving ?D
C: category
D: display_map_class C
disp_functor (functor_identity C) ?D (disp_codomain C)
C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (c c' : C) (f : C ⟦ c', c ⟧) (d : ?D c),
is_cartesian (♯ ?χ (?clD c c' f d))

  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
disp_cat C
 exact (display_map_cat D).
  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
cleaving (display_map_cat D)
 exact display_map_cleaving.
  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
disp_functor (functor_identity C) (display_map_cat D)
  (disp_codomain C)
 exact (ι D).
  
C: category
D: display_map_class C
∏ (c c' : C) (f : C ⟦ c', c ⟧)
(d : display_map_cat D c),
is_cartesian (♯ (ι D) (display_map_cleaving c c' f d))
 exact ι_preserves_cartesian.
Defined.
Notation "'DM2CC'" := display_map_to_comprehension_category : disp_map_cat.

disp_nat_trans_axioms
  ((λ (x : C₁) (dx : display_map_cat_data D₁ x),
    id_disp (display_map_functor F x dx))
   :
   disp_nat_trans_data (λ c : C₁, identity (F c))
     (disp_functor_composite_data (π_χ (DM2CC D₁))
        (disp_codomain_functor F))
     (disp_functor_composite_data
        (display_map_functor F) (π_χ (DM2CC D₂))))
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂
F: display_map_class_functor D₁ D₂
y, x: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ y, x ⟧
dy: display_map_cat_data D₁ y
dx: display_map_cat_data D₁ x
ff: dy -->[ f] dx
(♯ (disp_functor_composite_data (π_χ (DM2CC D₁))
      (disp_codomain_functor F)) ff ;; id_disp
                                         (display_map_functor
                                            F x dx))%mor_disp =
transportb
  (mor_disp
     (disp_functor_composite_data (π_χ (DM2CC D₁))
        (disp_codomain_functor F) y dy)
     (disp_functor_composite_data
        (display_map_functor F) (π_χ (DM2CC D₂)) x dx))
  (nat_trans_ax (nat_trans_id F) y x f)
  (id_disp (display_map_functor F y dy) ;; ♯ (disp_functor_composite_data
                                                (display_map_functor
                                                 F)
                                                (π_χ
                                                 (DM2CC
                                                 D₂)))
                                             ff)%mor_disp
 
C₁, C₂: category
D₁: display_map_class C₁
D₂: display_map_class C₂

y, x: C₁
f: C₁ ⟦ y, x ⟧
dy: display_map_cat_data D₁ y
dx: display_map_cat_data D₁ x
ff: dy -->[ f] dx
(((# F)%cat (pr1 ff),,
  disp_codomain_functor_data_subproof C₁ C₂ F y x
    (pr1 dy,, pr12 dy) (pr1 dx,, pr12 dx) f ff) ;; 
 id_disp
   (F (pr1 dx),,
    (# F)%cat (pr12 dx),,
    (pr12 F) (pr1 dx) x (pr12 dx) (pr22 dx)))%mor_disp =
transportb
  (mor_disp (F (pr1 dy),, # F (pr12 dy))
     (F (pr1 dx),, # F (pr12 dx)))
  (is_nat_trans_id F y x f)
  (id_disp
     (F (pr1 dy),,
      (# F)%cat (pr12 dy),,
      (pr12 F) (pr1 dy) y (pr12 dy) (pr22 dy)) ;; 
   ((# F)%cat (pr1 ff),,
    display_map_functor_data_subproof C₁ C₂ D₁ D₂ F y
      x dy dx f ff))%mor_disp

   # F (pr12 dy) · (# F f · identity (F x)))

C₁, C₂: category

        (internal_paths_rew_r (C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 dx), F x ⟧)
           (# F (pr12 dx) · identity (F x))
           (# F (pr12 dx))
           (λ p : C₂ ⟦ F (pr1 dx), F x ⟧,
            # F (pr12 dx) = p)
           (idpath (# F (pr12 dx)))
           (id_right (# F (pr12 dx))))
        (id_left (# F (pr12 dx))))
     (identity (F (pr1 dx)),,
      disp_map_id_comp_subproof C₂ D₂ (F x)
        (F (pr1 dx),,
         # F (pr12 dx),,
         (pr12 F) (pr1 dx) x (pr12 dx) (pr22 dx)))) =
pr1
  (identity (F (pr1 dx)),,
   cod_id_comp_subproof C₂ (F x)
     (F (pr1 dx),, # F (pr12 dx)))

identity (F (pr1 dx)) · identity (F (pr1 dx)) =
identity (F (pr1 dx))

        exact (id_left _).

Notation "'MD2PM'" := map_display_map_to_pseudo_map_structure : disp_map_cat.

(** ** Transformation corresponding to a natural transformation between functors between display map categories *)


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F, F': display_map_class_functor D D'
α: F ⟹ F'
transformation_structure_axiom
  (display_map_nat_trans α)


C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F, F': display_map_class_functor D D'
α: F ⟹ F'
transformation_structure_axiom
  (display_map_nat_trans α)

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F, F': display_map_class_functor D D'
α: F ⟹ F'
x: C
xx: pr1 (DM2CC D) x
((pr22 (MD2PM F)) x xx ;; ♯ (π_χ (DM2CC D'))
                            (display_map_nat_trans α x
                               xx))%mor_disp =
transportb
  (λ f : C' ⟦ pr1 (MD2PM F) x,
         functor_identity C' (pr1 (MD2PM F') x) ⟧,
   disp_codomain_functor (pr1 (MD2PM F))
     (functor_identity C x) (π_χ (DM2CC D) x xx) -->[
   f] disp_functor_composite (pr12 (MD2PM F'))
        (π_χ (DM2CC D')) x xx) (mor_base_equal α x)
  (disp_codomain_nat_trans α (functor_identity C x)
     (π_χ (DM2CC D) x xx) ;; (pr22 (MD2PM F')) x xx)%mor_disp

  
C, C': category
D: display_map_class C
D': display_map_class C'
F, F': display_map_class_functor D D'
α: F ⟹ F'
x: C
xx: pr1 (DM2CC D) x
pr1
  ((pr22 (MD2PM F)) x xx ;; ♯ (π_χ (DM2CC D'))
                              (display_map_nat_trans α
                                 x xx))%mor_disp =
pr1
  (transportb
     (λ f : C' ⟦ pr1 (MD2PM F) x,
            functor_identity C' (pr1 (MD2PM F') x) ⟧,
      disp_codomain_functor (pr1 (MD2PM F))
        (functor_identity C x) (π_χ (DM2CC D) x xx) -->[
      f] disp_functor_composite (pr12 (MD2PM F'))
           (π_χ (DM2CC D')) x xx) (mor_base_equal α x)
     (disp_codomain_nat_trans α (functor_identity C x)
        (π_χ (DM2CC D) x xx) ;; (pr22 (MD2PM F')) x xx)%mor_disp)

  exact (idpath _).
Qed.
